BEHEN CHDO K BACHE MAA K LODE

TU LAR AAAA B EHEN K LODE
RHA HON YAHAN

KO MAA DARCHDU TERI BEAHN KI CHUT MN TIME BOMB

FIT MARO BEAHN KLURE TERI BEAHN KI CHUT MN MACHINE

GUN FIT KR K US KO JUNGAL MN CHOR DO MAA K LURE

FEEL KR BEAHN CHDU TERI BEAHN KI CHUT HY YAHAN

KO MAA DARCHDU TERI BEAHN KI NON STOP CHUDI MAR

RHA HON YAHAN KO BEHAN KLURE TERI EBAHN KI CHUT

MARO BEHAN CHUD TERI BEAHN KO NAGA KR K CHUDO MAA DARCHUD

KUTTI MAA KI NASAL BEAHN CHDU TERI BEAHN

KI CHUT MN LAN DO MAA DARCHUD

YAHAN KO TERI BEAHN CHUD RAHI HY

OR TOU EK HY K APNE CHUTI BEHAN KI

CHUDI V MERE SE KRNA CHALA HY BEAHN

CHDU TERI EBAHN KI CHUT HY YAHAN KO

MAA DARCHUD SALI BEAHN KO MN NE PECHPAN

SE CHUDA Y MAA DARCHUD WO MERA LAN LE LE

KR SIKH GAI HY
EHEN CHOD KA BCEH KTUE KA BCEH

BEHEN CHDO K BCHE MAA K LODE DALI KB ACEH

TIER BEHEN KO CHOD
TERI BEHAEN KI CHOT EM LUN MARON E
 KI CHUT MN LAN DE KR US KO MAR

DO MAA K LURE TERI BEAHN KI CHUT MN LAN PHASA KR RAKHA HOWA HY MN NE BEAHN CHDU

A KR APNE BEAHN KI LIVE CHUDI DEKH KE BEHAN

CHDU TERI BEAHN KO ZOR ZOR SE CHUD RHA HON US

KI TATTI BAHAR KO A KR LAG RAHI HY BEHAN K LURE

RHA HON YAHAN

KO MAA DARCHDU TERI BEAHN KI CHUT MN TIME BOMB

FIT MARO BEAHN KLURE TERI BEAHN KI CHUT MN MACHINE

GUN FIT KR K US KO JUNGAL MN CHOR DO MAA K LURE

FEEL KR BEAHN CHDU TERI BEAHN KI CHUT HY YAHAN

KO MAA DARCHDU TERI BEAHN KI NON STOP CHUDI MAR

RHA HON YAHAN KO BEHAN KLURE TERI EBAHN KI CHUT

MARO BEHAN CHUD TERI BEAHN KO NAGA KR K CHUDO MAA DARCHUD

KUTTI MAA KI NASAL BEAHN CHDU TERI BEAHN

KI CHUT MN LAN DO MAA DARCHUD

YAHAN KO TERI BEAHN CHUD RAHI HY

OR TOU EK HY K APNE CHUTI BEHAN KI

TERI BEEN KI CHOT MARON GAHEN

SALE BEHEN CHOD KB ACHEMA K LODE

TERI BEHEN KI CHOT MAROGA HEN

TERI BEHEN KA PHUDA MARON

KUTE K BACEH BEHEN K LODE

BEHEN CHOD KBACHEMA K LODE

TERI EBHEN KI KUS MARON ME

SAEL BEHEN CHOD BACEH AM K LDOE

TERI BEHEN KI CHUT

MAA K LOREY SALETERI MA AKI KUSS MARU LOREYT
TERI MAA KI CHOOT CHOD  DU
MAA K LAND SALEY BHOSDE
TERI MA AKI CHUT MARU DALEY

SALE BEHEN CHDO ABCHE MA K LDOE

TER BEHEN KI CHOT HEN
